### Removed



## [0.25.0] - 2026-05-03



> Pre-ingest triage workflow (#845): sidecar issue cache + JSONL audit log + accept/reject/defer/needs-AC state machine + bulk ops + pre-swarm freshness gate + refinement Phase 0 + idempotent bootstrap. Six story PRs landed via swarm cascade.



### Added

- **feat(triage): local issue cache + #583 quarantine (#845 Story 1)** -- introduces a sidecar issue cache at `.deft-cache/issues/<owner>-<repo>/<N>.{json,md}` so the refinement / triage pipeline stops paying O(N) `gh issue view` calls per evaluation pass (the #788 token-cost adoption blocker). Wave-1 deliverable for the #845 epic, owned by Agent A1; non-overlapping with the parallel A2 candidates-audit-log story. New `scripts/triage_cache.py` exposes the canonical public surface (`populate(repo, force=False) -> int`, `show(issue_number, repo) -> str`, `is_stale(path, ttl_seconds) -> bool`); populate uses `gh issue list --state open --json number,title,body,...` (or the optional `gitcrawl` backend when `--use-gitcrawl` is passed and the binary is on PATH), atomic-replace per-issue writes via `os.replace` so torn files cannot leak into a parallel reader, and an mtime-based 24h freshness gate (`DEFAULT_TTL_SECONDS`) so re-runs are idempotent and skip fresh entries (mtime preserved on no-change, `--force` opts back into a full re-write). New `scripts/quarantine_ext.py` exposes `quarantine_body(raw_md: str) -> str` per the #583 prompt-injection-quarantine spec: markdown headings or plain-prose lines containing imperative tokens (`STEP`, `TASK:`, `IMPORTANT:`, `MUST`, `SYSTEM:`, `IGNORE PREVIOUS`, ...) are wrapped in ```quarantined fenced code blocks so a downstream agent splicing the cached body into a turn payload sees a syntactic marker, not executable instructions; idempotent on re-run; respects existing fenced code blocks so heading-shaped prose inside ``` is left alone; word-boundary scoped so `stepladder` does not match `STEP`. New standalone `tasks/triage-cache.yml` Taskfile fragment exposes `triage:cache` and `triage:show` targets (no `sources:` / `generates:` per `conventions/task-caching.md` since both surface user-facing flags via `{{.CLI_ARGS}}`); the parent `Taskfile.yml` `includes:` wiring is intentionally NOT performed here -- that surface is owned by Story 6 (Agent A6). New `tests/test_triage_cache.py` (28+ tests across 6 sections) covers the five Test-narrative cases: (1) populate from gh fixture writes both `<N>.json` and `<N>.md` per issue; (2) re-populate is idempotent (mtime preserved); (3) quarantine wraps suspicious content per #583 (heading + inline directive variants, code-block guard, word-boundary guard); (4) gitcrawl absent -> graceful fallback to gh (default `use_gitcrawl=None` always picks gh; explicit `use_gitcrawl=True` against missing gitcrawl raises `TriageCacheError`); (5) malformed `--repo` -> friendly `InvalidRepoError` with parametrized coverage of empty / single-segment / trailing-slash / triple-segment / whitespace forms; CLI surface returns 2 on arg error mirroring argparse convention. `.gitignore` appended with `.deft-cache/` so the local mirror is never versioned. Refs #845 (epic remains OPEN until all 6 stories ship); refs #583 (quarantine spec consumer); refs #788 (token-cost root cause).

- **feat(triage): candidates.jsonl audit log + JSON schema (#845 Story 2)** -- ships the append-only triage decision audit trail at `vbrief/.eval/candidates.jsonl` plus its frozen JSON Schema 2020-12 contract at `vbrief/schemas/candidates.schema.json`. Each line is a single JSON object capturing one decision with required fields `decision_id` (UUID), `timestamp` (ISO-8601 UTC), `repo` (`owner/name`), `issue_number` (int), `decision` (enum: `accept` | `reject` | `defer` | `needs-ac` | `mark-duplicate` | `reset`), and `actor`; optional `reason`; conditional `linked_to` (required iff `decision=mark-duplicate`) and `prior_decision_id` (required iff `decision=reset`). Schema is the FROZEN downstream contract consumed by Story 3 (triage actions), Story 4 (`triage:bulk` + `triage:refresh`), and Story 6 (bootstrap). New `scripts/candidates_log.py` exposes the public surface `append(entry) -> decision_id`, `read_all(repo=None) -> list[dict]`, `find_by_issue(issue_number, repo) -> list[dict]`, `latest_decision(issue_number, repo) -> dict | None` plus a `new_decision_id()` UUID helper; the writer is append-only (never rewrites existing lines), schema-validates every entry via a hand-rolled mirror of the JSON Schema (no third-party `jsonschema` dep required), creates the `.eval/` parent directory on first write, and is concurrent-append safe via a stdlib advisory lock (`msvcrt.locking` on Windows / `fcntl.flock` on POSIX) plus a module-level `threading.Lock` that serialises in-process writers so the line-level atomicity holds even when the OS-level byte-range lock is granted to multiple file descriptors held by the same process. Reader tolerates malformed lines (logs a warning, skips) so a partially-written tail from a crashed appender never bricks the audit trail. New `tests/test_candidates_log.py` covers all five Test-narrative cases -- append+read round-trip, malformed-line tolerance, 8-thread x 25-append concurrent stress, schema rejection of every required-field / conditional-dependency violation, and `latest_decision` sorting by timestamp rather than insertion order -- plus a happy-path test for `mark-duplicate` + `reset` conditional fields and a UUID-helper smoke test. Programmatic library only -- the user-facing `task triage:*` surface lands in Story 3.

- **feat(skills): refinement Phase 0 -- pre-ingest triage workflow (#845 Story 5)** -- extends `skills/deft-directive-refinement/SKILL.md` with a new Phase 0 (Triage -- Cache + Action Menu) inserted before the existing Phase 1 -- Ingest. Phase 0 is the canonical pre-ingest entry point introduced under #845: it operates on the three-tier inventory model (`.deft-cache/issues/` local mirror + `vbrief/.eval/candidates.jsonl` audit log + `vbrief/proposed/` accepted-only) and walks each cached candidate through a deterministic action menu (`accept | reject | defer | needs-ac | mark-duplicate`, with `Discuss` and `Back` as the final two numbered options per `contracts/deterministic-questions.md`) so that **only user-accepted items reach `vbrief/proposed/`**, eliminating the pre-#845 ingest-everything-then-evaluate drift in the proposed/ folder. Each menu option routes to the canonical `task triage:*` commands introduced under Stories 1-4 (`task triage:cache` / `task triage:bootstrap` / `task triage:accept` / `task triage:reject` / `task triage:defer` / `task triage:needs-ac` / `task triage:mark-duplicate` / `task triage:bulk` / `task triage:refresh`); skills MUST NOT reimplement the audit-log append, schema validation, or proposed/ write inline (mirrors the #537 ingest-task discipline). **Auto-skip:** when `.deft-cache/issues/` is missing/empty AND `vbrief/.eval/candidates.jsonl` is empty-of-non-terminals, Phase 0 emits the verbatim informational message `triage cache empty -- skipping Phase 0; opt in via \`task triage:bootstrap\`` and chains directly into Phase 1 without prompting -- consumers without a populated cache see no behavioral change. The legacy `## Phase 0 -- Branch Setup` block is renamed to `## Branch Setup (Preflight)` and remains as a preflight gate ahead of Phase 0; existing Phase 1+ semantics (Ingest / Evaluate / Reconcile / Promote-Demote / Prioritize / Completion Lifecycle) are preserved verbatim. Cross-references updated: `## When to Use` advertises Phase 0 as the new entry point and points at `contracts/deterministic-questions.md`; the new `**See also**` banner near the top of the skill links the deterministic-questions contract and the new triage task surface; the `## Deterministic Questions Contract` block is extended to cover the Phase 0 action menu; the `## Session Model` bullet list gains a Phase 0 trigger row; three new ⊗ Phase 0 anti-patterns join the existing Anti-Patterns block (don't bypass Tier 1 / don't skip the audit log / don't skip Phase 1 silently). Single-file owner: `skills/deft-directive-refinement/SKILL.md` (per the Agent A5 vBRIEF at `vbrief/active/2026-05-03-845-triage-refinement-phase-0.vbrief.json`). Doc-only -- no script, task, or schema changes ship with this story; those are owned by Stories 1-4 + 6 of the same epic. Refs #845.

- **feat(triage): action commands (#845 Story 3)** -- per-issue triage decision surface implementing the 8 actions from the Story 3 Overview narrative: `accept(N, repo)`, `reject(N, repo, reason)`, `defer(N, repo)`, `needs_ac(N, repo)`, `mark_duplicate(N, repo, of_n)`, `status(N, repo)`, `reset(N, repo)`, `history(N, repo)`. New `scripts/triage_actions.py` consumes the frozen Story 1 cache surface (`triage_cache.show`) for mark-duplicate target validation and the frozen Story 2 audit-log surface (`candidates_log.append` / `latest_decision` / `find_by_issue`) for decision recording. Reject closes the upstream GitHub issue via `gh issue close <N> --comment '<reason>' --reason 'not planned'` AND applies the `triage-rejected` label; on gh failure the companion audit entry is rolled back via a JSONL line-filter rewrite so the trail never references a decision that did not actually take effect. Reset is reversible -- it appends a `reset` entry whose `prior_decision_id` points at the most recent non-reset decision; history is NEVER deleted. All actions are idempotent on already-final state (re-rejecting a rejected issue is a no-op, not an error). New `tasks/triage-actions.yml` is a STANDALONE Taskfile fragment (NOT yet wired into the parent `Taskfile.yml` -- Story 6 owns that integration) exposing `triage:accept`, `triage:reject`, `triage:defer`, `triage:needs-ac`, `triage:mark-duplicate`, `triage:status`, `triage:reset`, `triage:history`; per `conventions/task-caching.md` no `sources:` / `generates:` because every target accepts user-facing flags via `{{.CLI_ARGS}}`. New `tests/test_triage_actions.py` covers all 10 cases enumerated in the Story 3 Test narrative (accept happy path; reject upstream-close + label success; defer; needs-ac with AC-request comment; mark-duplicate cache-validation rejection then success; status latest; history timestamp ordering; reset chain depth >= 2 referencing prior; reject upstream-close failure rolls audit entry back; idempotent re-action no-op) using `monkeypatch.setattr` fakes for the upstream `candidates_log` and `triage_cache` modules so the suite is hermetic. Refs #845 (Story 3 of 6).

- **feat(triage): bulk ops + freshness gate (#845 Story 4)** -- introduces `scripts/triage_bulk.py` (four bulk actions `bulk-accept` / `bulk-reject` / `bulk-defer` / `bulk-needs-ac`, combinable AND-semantics filter flags `--label` / `--author` / `--age-days` / `--cluster`, looping internally through Story 3's single-issue actions; zero-match exits clean) and `scripts/triage_refresh.py` (the pre-swarm freshness gate `task triage:refresh-active`: walks `vbrief/active/*.vbrief.json`, compares cached vs live `gh issue view <N> --json updatedAt`, surfaces drift via a three-way prompt `proceed-with-stale` / `refresh-and-update-local` / `defer-from-this-batch`; empty active is a no-op; `proceed-with-stale` records an audit annotation via Story 2's `candidates_log`). Ships the standalone `tasks/triage-bulk.yml` Taskfile fragment exposing `triage:bulk-accept` / `triage:bulk-reject` / `triage:bulk-defer` / `triage:bulk-needs-ac` / `triage:refresh-active` (NOT yet wired into parent `Taskfile.yml`; that include is owned by Story 6). New `tests/test_triage_bulk.py` covers the bulk-accept --label fixture, combined `--label --age-days` AND-filter, and zero-match clean exit; new `tests/test_triage_refresh.py` covers empty-active no-op, single-drift three-way prompt rendering with mocked input, and the proceed-with-stale audit-annotation contract. Upstream Story 1 (`triage_cache`), Story 2 (`candidates_log`), and Story 3 (`triage_actions`) modules are imported lazily so this story PR is mergeable independently of upstream landing order; tests inject stubs via dependency-injection seams. The freshness primitive introduced here is consumed by `#868` (lock-comment protocol). **Post-rebase fix (Greptile P1 on PR #875):** after #874 (Story 1) and #876 (Story 2) merged ahead of this story, the previously-stubbed `candidates_log` became real and its frozen `_validate_entry` rejected the `freshness-annotation` decision (not in the `{accept,reject,defer,needs-ac,mark-duplicate,reset}` enum) AND the missing-required `decision_id` field, raising `CandidatesLogError` (`ValueError` subclass) every time a user picked `proceed-with-stale`. `scripts/triage_refresh.py::_record_audit_annotation` now (a) generates a UUID4 `decision_id` via `candidates_log.new_decision_id()` (UUID fallback when the helper is absent) so the required-fields portion of the schema is satisfied, and (b) wraps `append()` in `try/except ValueError` so a schema mismatch degrades to a stderr `WARN` line rather than crashing the CLI -- the `proceed-with-stale (audit recorded)` stdout signal is still emitted by the caller and the operator now sees a clear pointer (`extend the Story 2 schema to capture it`) for the follow-up. Two new `tests/test_triage_refresh.py` regressions pin the contract: schema-rejection -> WARN-and-continue, and helper-absent -> UUID4 fallback. Also fixes the post-rebase mypy CI regression at `tests/test_triage_bulk.py:233` (`int(args[0])` against `*args: object` -- changed to `*args: Any`). Refs `#845`, refs `#868`.

- **feat(scripts,tasks,docs): triage v1 bootstrap + parent Taskfile wiring + UPGRADING migration + privacy + quarantine specs (#845 Story 6)** -- closes the LAST story in the #845 cascade. Adds `scripts/triage_bootstrap.py`, an idempotent five-step installer reachable via `task triage:bootstrap`: (1) populate `.deft-cache/issues/<owner>-<repo>/` for all open upstream issues by delegating to Story 1's `scripts.triage_cache.populate` (graceful no-op when Story 1 hasn't merged yet); (2) backfill `vbrief/.eval/candidates.jsonl` with one `accepted` audit entry per scope vBRIEF currently in `vbrief/proposed/` / `vbrief/pending/` / `vbrief/active/` -- intentionally skipping `vbrief/cancelled/` so rejected items are NOT reanimated; the backfill prefers Story 2's `scripts.candidates_log.append` advisory-locked write surface when available, and falls back to a self-contained JSONL append matching the same schema; (3) append `.deft-cache/` to `.gitignore` when absent (NFR-1 default-on per `docs/privacy-nfr.md`); (4) best-effort `pipx install gitcrawl` when neither gitcrawl nor a previous install is on PATH; (5) recap with the canonical next commands. Three-state exit (0 success, 1 step failure, 2 config error) mirrors `scripts/preflight_branch.py` (#747). Adds `tasks/triage-bootstrap.yml` as a standalone Taskfile fragment exposing an inner `bootstrap` task wired into the parent Taskfile via the new `triage-bootstrap` include namespace; the parent `Taskfile.yml` `includes:` block also references the three sibling fragments (`tasks/triage-cache.yml` from Story 1, `tasks/triage-actions.yml` from Story 3, `tasks/triage-bulk.yml` from Story 4) under unique `triage-cache` / `triage-actions` / `triage-bulk` namespaces (each `optional: true` so the cascade tolerates rolling merges) plus a top-level alias `triage:bootstrap` delegating to `triage-bootstrap:bootstrap` so the user-facing `task triage:bootstrap` form documented in `UPGRADING.md` and the vBRIEF resolves. `UPGRADING.md` gains a new `## Migration to triage v1` section at the top following the canonical four-field micro-format header (`Applies when` / `Safe to auto-run` / `Restart required` / `Commands`) documenting additive nature, ~5-minute opt-in path, gitignore default + opt-in commit-cache contract, the rollback recipe, and cross-references to the two new docs. New `docs/quarantine-spec.md` formalizes the #583 injection-quarantine algorithm consumed by Story 1's cache writer (input, four-step heuristic on heading-imperative tokens like `STEP`/`TASK:`/`IMPORTANT:`, fence info string `quarantined`, idempotency, security rationale, plus three escape-hatch overrides: `--allow-tokens`, the `<!-- quarantine: skip -->` per-issue bypass, and `--force-quarantine`). New `docs/privacy-nfr.md` codifies five non-functional requirements: gitignore default-on (NFR-1), opt-in commit-cache path requiring deliberate `.gitignore` edit (NFR-2), local-only at rest with no telemetry (NFR-3), private-repo body content treatment (NFR-4), and user-data classification for GDPR/CCPA audits (NFR-5). New `tests/test_triage_bootstrap.py` (six cases per the vBRIEF Test narrative) covers fresh-project end-to-end, re-run idempotency (zero duplicate audit entries on second pass), backfill-respects-lifecycle-folders, cancelled-not-reanimated, gitcrawl-already-installed-noop, and parent-Taskfile-includes-wired (PyYAML parse + defence-in-depth grep over the four fragment file paths). Tests are hermetic via `unittest.mock.patch` over `shutil.which` so they run without a real `pipx` / `gitcrawl` binary on PATH. Closes #845 Story 6; merges LAST in the cascade per the parent monitor's sequencing.

### Added

- **docs(upgrading): document AGENTS.md managed-section legacy migration contract (#794)** -- closes the adoption-blocker docs gap surfaced by issue #794. New `## From pre-#768 AGENTS.md → managed-section AGENTS.md` section in `UPGRADING.md` carries the canonical four-field micro-format header (`Applies when` / `Safe to auto-run` / `Restart required` / `Commands`) and documents (a) the detection rule -- `./AGENTS.md` exists but lacks the `<!-- deft:managed-section v1 -->` / `<!-- /deft:managed-section -->` sentinel markers (gate output `agents-md=missing`); (b) the **one-time legacy migration**: `deft/run agents:refresh` preserves existing AGENTS.md content verbatim ABOVE the rendered managed section (one-blank-line separator), so consumer notes survive the migration intact; (c) the four-state taxonomy classified by `_classify_agents_md` (`current` / `stale` / `missing` / `absent`) with the action taken on each; (d) the long-term **sentinel-only-rewrite contract**: every subsequent `deft/run agents:refresh` reads only the bytes between the markers and replaces them in place when the rendered template drifts, never touching content above or below the bracketed region; (e) cross-references to `templates/agents-entry.md` (the rendered managed-section template -- the bytes the framework writes between the markers) and `QUICK-START.md` Case G (agent-prescriptive coverage of the same scenario for agents reading QUICK-START.md instead of running `agents:refresh` directly). New `tests/content/test_upgrading_sections.py::test_managed_section_legacy_migration_section_present` regression-pins the contract surface area: section presence, detection-rule tokens (`<!-- deft:managed-section v1 -->`, `agents-md=missing`), command (`deft/run agents:refresh`), behavior tokens (`one-time`, `sentinel-only`), and both cross-references. The pre-existing `test_every_section_has_four_field_header` assertion automatically covers the new section's four-field header. Pure-docs PR -- no changes to `run`, `templates/agents-entry.md`, or `QUICK-START.md`. Closes #794.

- **feat(tasks/migrate): add `task migrate:preflight` aggregate; `migrate:vbrief` self-invokes it (#793)** -- closes the adoption blocker where consumers running `task migrate:vbrief` directly (not via the agent-driven setup skill) got no preflight checks and hit raw subprocess failures (`uv` not found, `FileNotFoundError`) with no remediation pointer. New `scripts/migrate_preflight.py` (pure stdlib + `subprocess`, three-state exit 0 ready / 1 not-ready / 2 config-error mirroring `scripts/preflight_branch.py` (#747) and `scripts/preflight_implementation.py` (#810)) reifies the prose contract from `skills/deft-directive-setup/SKILL.md` § Environment Preflight as a runnable task. Three checks: (1) `uv` on PATH (FAIL with `https://docs.astral.sh/uv/` pointer if missing); (2) v0.20+ layout -- `<deft-root>/scripts/migrate_vbrief.py` and `<deft-root>/vbrief/schemas/` must exist (FAIL if missing) and `<project>/vbrief/` (WARN-only when missing -- greenfield projects get it created on first run); (3) git working-tree state -- a dirty tree is reported as WARN (the migrator's own dirty-tree guard fires with an actionable `--force` pointer; double-blocking would be redundant and would break the recommended `task migrate:vbrief -- --dry-run` preview path), non-git directories are also WARN-level skips rather than FAIL. New `tasks/migrate.yml::preflight` Taskfile target dispatches the helper (no `sources:` / `generates:` per `conventions/task-caching.md`); `tasks/migrate.yml::vbrief` gains a `deps: [task: preflight]` declaration so any non-zero preflight exit aborts the run before any destructive mutation. Soft-dep on #792 (`cmd_doctor` uv-detection helper) noted in module docstring -- a local `_uv_available()` is defined here for now to keep this PR self-contained; when #792 lands a future small follow-up can DRY both surfaces. UTF-8 stdout/stderr self-reconfigure at `main()` entry per #814 so the gate's status lines render under Windows cp1252 default. New `tests/cli/test_migrate_preflight.py` (22 tests across primitive checks, `evaluate()` aggregate, and `main()` CLI surface) covers the three exit states with `shutil.which` and `subprocess.run` patched per test so the suite is hermetic and host-independent: exit 0 (all PASS / WARN-only path including dirty-tree WARN), exit 1 (uv missing FAIL / framework migrator FAIL / framework schemas FAIL / multiple-FAIL aggregation), exit 2 (`--project-root` missing / `--project-root` is a file / `--deft-root` missing); plus per-primitive tests for the layout WARN-when-greenfield surface and a `--quiet` smoke test. Closes #793.

- **feat(scripts,tasks,hooks,docs): deterministic-tier PS 5.1 non-ASCII corruption gate (#798)** -- closes the adoption-blocker recurrence pattern that bit Windows consumers in their first session four times before this fix landed (#236 t1.11.1, #240 t1.11.2, #283 t1.20.1, PR #795 / 2026-05-01 -- a maintainer with all three prose rules loaded corrupted 132 lines of `CHANGELOG.md`). Per `main.md` Rule Authority [AXIOM] this elevates the rule from prose tier to deterministic tier. New `scripts/verify_encoding.py` (pure stdlib, mirrors `scripts/preflight_branch.py` shape with the #814 UTF-8 self-reconfigure block at `main()` entry) scans tracked text files for U+FFFD replacement chars, the curated CP1252-as-UTF-8 / CP437-as-UTF-8 mojibake bigram set (cp1252 forms covering the recurrence record #236/#240/#283/#795; cp437 forms covering the PR #844 / fix #846 record), and unexpected UTF-8 BOM on .md/.json/.yml/.yaml/.txt. Three-state exit (0 clean / 1 corruption with `path:line:[label] context` diagnostic / 2 config error). Mode flags `--all` (default; aggregated into `task check`) and `--staged` (`.githooks/pre-commit` invocation, runs after the existing #747 branch-protection step). False-positive guards: markdown inline-code spans (single backticks) and fenced code blocks are stripped before scanning .md files so recurrence-record prose can quote the bigrams without flagging itself; built-in allow-list skips the #798 brief itself across every lifecycle folder + `history/archive/**` (preserved historical state); `--allow-list <path>` accepts a newline-separated glob file for project-specific documented exceptions. New `tasks/verify.yml::encoding` Taskfile target wraps the script (NO `sources:` / `generates:` per `conventions/task-caching.md` -- user-facing flags MUST NOT be silently swallowed by go-task's incremental-build cache, mirroring the `task release` (#74) and `task pr:check-protected-issues` (#702) precedents); wired into the `task check` aggregate at `Taskfile.yml::check.deps` between `verify:branch` and `vbrief:validate`. `.githooks/pre-commit` extended to dispatch `verify_encoding.py --staged` after `preflight_branch.py`, mirroring the `${DEFT_PYTHON:-python3}` discovery + `python3` / `python` fallback already in the hook. AGENTS.md `## PowerShell` section rewritten with the root-cause rule covering BOTH reads and writes (`Get-Content -Raw` decodes via the active Windows codepage on the READ side BEFORE any safe write can preserve the bytes; PS 7+ / bash / zsh exempt) plus the four-recurrence record AND the personal-rule cross-reference (`3MieNBQjwlObZM1If060iy`). New `tests/cli/test_verify_encoding.py` parametrizes regression coverage over the full mojibake bigram set (one test per pattern), U+FFFD detection, BOM-on-.md / BOM-on-.json positive cases vs BOM-on-.ps1 negative case, the markdown inline-code false-positive guard (the recurrence-record case where mojibake appears legitimately inside backticks), `--allow-list` bypass, three-state exit codes (0 / 1 / 2), `--staged` mode against a synthetic git index built in `tmp_path`, and the built-in allow-list (vBRIEF self-reference + history/archive). New `meta/lessons.md` cross-reference (`## PS 5.1 Non-ASCII Round-Trip Corruption -- elevated to deterministic tier (2026-05)`) follows the Rule Authority [AXIOM] strongest-applicable-layer pattern -- the rule body lives in the gate + AGENTS.md, NOT duplicated in prose. Closes #798.

- **feat(gate): periodic remote-version probe via `git ls-remote` with 24h-per-tag throttle (#801)** -- closes the adoption blocker where directive had zero awareness of upstream releases. New `cmd_check_updates` in `run` (registered as `check-updates` in the dispatcher and added to `_UPGRADE_GATE_SKIP_COMMANDS` so it does not recursively re-trigger the gate) runs a read-only `git ls-remote --tags --refs <upstream>` probe -- resolving upstream from the consumer's `./deft` submodule's `origin` remote (or the run-rooted repo's origin when invoked from inside the framework checkout) -- parses the highest semver tag, and compares it to the in-process `VERSION`. Six output statuses (`OK` / `BEHIND` / `NO-UPSTREAM` / `NO-TAGS` / `ERROR` / `SKIPPED`) with a `--json` variant; exit code is 1 only on positive BEHIND so `task framework:check-updates` returns non-zero in CI when an upstream release is available. Honors `DEFT_NO_NETWORK=1` (silent skip before any subprocess call), `DEFT_REMOTE_PROBE_TIMEOUT` (default 5s, env-overridable), and `DEFT_FORCE_REMOTE_PROBE=1` (bypass throttle for the `task framework:check-updates -- --force` recovery flag). Throttle helpers (`_read_remote_probe_state` / `_write_remote_probe_state`) persist `vbrief/.deft-remote-probe.json` with 24h probe / 24h notification cadence, per-tag re-notification (a fresh upstream tag re-fires immediately even if the prior tag was just dismissed), and a per-`run`-invocation dedup flag (`_PROBE_NOTIFIED_THIS_SESSION`) so chained commands do not stack identical banners. New `tasks/framework.yml` Taskfile entry `framework:check-updates` (with `--force` flag mapped to `DEFT_FORCE_REMOTE_PROBE=1` via go-task templating) wired into the root `Taskfile.yml` includes. Wired into `_check_upgrade_gate` AFTER the existing recorded-vs-current branch and the `agents-md:stale` emit -- the gate runs the probe on EVERY non-skip path (happy and unhappy) so a current-marker consumer still sees the upstream-drift signal, with a `needs_prompt` flag distinguishing local-drift (prompts) from remote-drift (informational only, never blocks CI). Three new test files (tests/cli/test_cmd_check_updates.py, tests/cli/test_remote_probe_throttle.py, tests/cli/test_upgrade_gate_remote_drift.py) cover all status outputs, exit codes, the `--json` variant, `DEFT_NO_NETWORK=1` short-circuit (verified via subprocess sentinel), malformed-tag handling, semver parser positive/negative cases, stable-outranks-prerelease ordering, cadence round-trip, 24h probe/notify floors, per-tag re-notification, per-session dedup, `DEFT_FORCE_REMOTE_PROBE=1` bypass, gate happy-path + unhappy-path integration with strict output ordering, no second prompt for remote drift only, and probe failure modes never breaking the gate. Closes #801.

- **feat(events): `framework:remote-drift` event registered and emitted on positive probe (#801)** -- new detection-bound event in `events/registry.json` with the canonical payload contract (`project_root`, `current_version`, `remote_version`, `upstream_url`, `commits_behind`); the `commits_behind` axis is `null` by default since the read-only probe cannot determine it without a `git fetch`. New `detect_remote_drift(project_root, *, probe_result)` payload-builder in `scripts/_event_detect.py` mirrors `detect_agents_md_stale`'s shape -- returns the structured payload when `probe_result.status == "behind"`, `None` otherwise. The actual `git ls-remote` probe lives in `run::_run_remote_probe` (kept there so the framework's bootstrap entry point is not coupled to the events surface at import time, mirroring why `run::_emit_event_safe` lazy-imports `emit`). Emission flows through `_emit_event_safe('framework:remote-drift', payload)` from the gate-integration site whenever the probe returns BEHIND. Mirrors the #635 pattern (`agents-md:stale`, `version:drift`, `pre-cutover:detected`) so consumers subscribing via `DEFT_EVENT_LOG` get a single uniform record shape across all detection-bound surfaces. Refs #801, refs #635 epic.
